G2 Atom Relations

Generated from the Sage companion code. Relations are expanded in the bottom-perm-top basis.

Each displayed relation also includes its vertical flip.

Atom Notation

For each atom with domain word \(u\) and codomain word \(v\), write \(A_{u}^{v}:u\to v\). The flipped atom is written \(\overline{A_{u}^{v}}\). Tensor products are written with \(\otimes\), and crossings are \(\beta_{12}\) and \(\beta_{21}\).
